G	G2	PART I : LAND OWNERSHIP, LAND TRANSACTIONS, AND PROPERTY RIGHTS IN THE EXPANSION AREA	1	<p>   <span style="font-size:12px;">The survey has three parts. The first part asks questions about <strong>property ownership and rights</strong> in the expansion areas of the city, the second part focuses on <strong>land use regulations</strong>, and the third part focuses on the <strong>subdivision of land</strong> into residential plots. We are interested in the single answer that applies to <u>all or most</u> of the land in the<em><strong> Expansion Area</strong></em>. If a single answer does not apply to approximately 80% of the <u>land</u> in the expansion area, we will ask you to write a short note explaining the situation in your city. If a question does not make sense to you, we want to understand why so that we obtain accurate information for your city. </span></p>  <div>   <a class="various fancybox.iframe" href="https://www.google.com/maps/d/u/0/embed?mid=zMhLaSs1bI9M.kb6YVP5NkORw&z=10&ll=11.17847,76.68364"><button>View Map</button></a></div>  		en

G	G2	PART I : LAND OWNERSHIP, LAND TRANSACTIONS, AND PROPERTY RIGHTS IN THE EXPANSION AREA	1	<p>   <span style="font-size:12px;">The survey has three parts. The first part asks questions about <strong>property ownership and rights</strong> in the expansion areas of the city, the second part focuses on <strong>land use regulations</strong>, and the third part focuses on the <strong>subdivision of land</strong> into residential plots. We are interested in the single answer that applies to <u>all or most</u> of the land in the<em><strong> Expansion Area</strong></em>. If a single answer does not apply to approximately 80% of the <u>land</u> in the expansion area, we will ask you to write a short note explaining the situation in your city. G	G2	PART I : LAND OWNERSHIP, LAND TRANSACTIONS, AND PROPERTY RIGHTS IN THE EXPANSION AREA	1	<p>   <span style="font-size:12px;">The survey has three parts. G	G2	PARTIE I: DROIT DE PROPRIETE, OPERATIONS FONCIERES, ET DROIT DE PROPRIETE DANS LA ZONE D’ EXPANSION 	1	<p>   <span style="font-size:12px;">L'enquête est constituée de trois parties. La première partie pose des questions sur les droits de l’immobilier et la propriété foncière dans la region d’expansion urbaine de la ville, la seconde se concentre sur la règlementation territoriale, et la troisième regarde la division des terrains en parcelles résidentielles dans la region d’expansion urbaine. Nous sommes intéressés par la réponse unique qui s'applique à tous ou à la plupart des terrains d’expansion urbaine. Si une réponse unique ne s'applique pas à environ 80% du territoire de l’ expansion urbaine , nous vous demanderons d'écrire un courte explication. Si une question s’applique pas à votre ville, nous souhaiterions comprendre pourquoi, afin d'obtenir des informations pertinentes concernant votre ville.</span></p>  <div>   <a class="various fancybox.iframe" href="https://www.google.com/maps/d/embed?mid=zMhLaSs1bI9M.kj1WMtpu2kx8&z=10&ll=19.25072,72.68827"><button>View Map</button></a></div>  		fr

G	G2	BAGIAN I: KEPEMILIKAN LAHAN, TRANSAKSI LAHAN, DAN HAK-HAK PROPERTI DI AREA PERLUASAN	1	<p>   Survei ini terdiri atas tiga bagian. Bagian pertama menanyakan tentang <strong>kepemilikan dan hak properti</strong> di area perluasan kota, bagian kedua berfokus pada <strong>peraturan penggunaan lahan</strong>, dan yang ketiga berfokus pada <strong>pemecahan lahan</strong> menjadi sejumlah bidang tanah tempat tinggal. Kami menginginkan jawaban tunggal yang berlaku pada<u> semua atau sebagian besar</u> lahan di Area Perluasan. Jika jawaban tunggal tidak berlaku pada sekitar 80% <u>lahan</u> di area perluasan, kami minta agar Anda menuliskan catatan pendek yang menjelaskan situasi di kota Anda.</p>  <div>   <a class="various fancybox.iframe" href="https://www.google.com/maps/d/u/0/embed?mid=zMhLaSs1bI9M.kb6YVP5NkORw&z=10&ll=11.17847,76.68364"><button>View Map</button></a></div>  		id

G	G2	파트 I:확장 지역의 토지 소유권, 토지 거래 및 재산권	1	<p>   설문 조사는 세 부분으로 나뉘어집니다. 첫 번째 부분에서는 도시 확장 지역의 부동산 소유권 및 권리 에 대한 문의사항으로 구성되고, 두 번째 부분에서는 토지 이용 규제에 초점을 맞추며, 세 번째 부분에서는 주거용 구획으로의 토지 세분화에 초점을 맞춥니다.</p>  <p>   저희는 확장 지역내의 <u>모든 또는 대부분</u>의 토지에 적용되는 단일 답변에 관심을 가지고 있습니다. 단일 답변이 확장 지역 내 토지의 약 80% 에 적용되지 않을 경우, 저희는 귀하 도시의 상황을 설명하는 메모를 간략하게 작성하도록 요청드립니다.</p>  <p>   문제가 이해가 되지 않을 경우, 저희가 귀하의 도시에 대한 정확한 정보를 얻을 수 있도록 '왜?' 라는 측면을 이해하고자 합니다.</p>  <p>   질문은 경우에 따라 확장 지역이 아닌 도시의 <em>외곽 지역</em>을 가리킬 수도 있습니다. 외곽 지역은 확장 지역의 경계 내부 또는 외부의 토지, 즉 현재 최근의 도시/대도시 개발이 이루어지고 있는 지역을 가리킵니다. 그럼, 파트 I 부터 시작하도록 하겠습니다.</p>  <div>   <a class="various fancybox.iframe" href="https://www.google.com/maps/d/u/0/embed?mid=zMhLaSs1bI9M.kb6YVP5NkORw&z=10&ll=11.17847,76.68364"><button>View Map</button></a></div>  		ko

G	G2	<strong>PARTE I:</strong> A PROPRIEDADE DA TERRA, AS TRANSAÇÕES IMOBILIÁRIAS E DIREITOS DE PROPRIEDA	1	<p>   A pesquisa tem três partes. A primeira parte faz perguntas sobre a <strong>propriedade e direitos</strong> nas áreas de expansão da cidade, a segunda parte se concentra na <strong>regulação do uso do solo</strong>, e a terceira parte se concentra no <strong>loteamento</strong> em lotes residenciais.</p>  <p>   Estamos interessados ​em resposta única que se aplique a <u>todos ou à maior parte</u> dos terrenos localizados na <em><strong>Área de Expansão</strong></em>. Se a resposta única não se aplicar em cerca de 80% dos <u>terrenos</u> localizada na área de expansão, lhe solicitaremos que escreva uma pequena nota explicando a situação em sua cidade.</p>  <p>   Se uma pergunta não fizer sentido para você, queremos entender o porquê, para que possamos obter informações precisas sobre sua cidade.</p>  <p>   As perguntas podem, algumas vezes, se referir à periferia da cidade, em vez da Área de Expansão. A periferia se refere a terrenos dentro ou talvez fora do limite externo da Área de Expansão, ou seja, as áreas mais recentes onde o desenvolvimento da cidade/área metropolitana está ocorrendo.</p>  <div>   <a class="various fancybox.iframe" href="https://www.google.com/maps/d/u/0/embed?mid=zMhLaSs1bI9M.kb6YVP5NkORw&z=10&ll=11.17847,76.68364"><button>View Map</button></a></div>  		pt-BR

G	G2	PART I : LAND OWNERSHIP, LAND TRANSACTIONS, AND PROPERTY RIGHTS IN THE EXPANSION AREA	1	<p>   <span style="font-size:12px;">The survey has three parts. The first part asks questions about <strong>property ownership and rights</strong> in the expansion areas of the city, the second part focuses on <strong>land use regulations</strong>, and the third part focuses on the <strong>subdivision of land</strong> into residential plots. We are interested in the single answer that applies to <u>all or most</u> of the land in the<em><strong> Expansion Area</strong></em>. If a single answer does not apply to approximately 80% of the <u>land</u> in the expansion area, we will ask you to write a short note explaining the situation in your city. If a question does not make sense to you, we want to understand why so that we obtain accurate information for your city. </span></p>  <div>   <a class="various fancybox.iframe" href="https://www.google.com/maps/d/u/0/embed?mid=zMhLaSs1bI9M.kb6YVP5NkORw&z=10&ll=11.17847,76.68364"><button>View Map</button></a></div>  		ru

G	G2	I PARTE:PROPIEDAD DEL SUELO, TRANSACCIONES DE SUELO Y DERECHOS DE PROPIEDAD EN EL ÁREA DE EXPANSIÓ	1	<p>   <span style="font-size:12px;">Esta Encuesta tiene tres partes. En la primera parte se pregunta acerca de la <strong>propiedad y derechos prediales</strong> en las áreas de expansión de la ciudad. La segunda parte se centra en las<strong> normas de uso del suelo</strong>, y la tercera parte se centra en la <strong>subdivisión del suelo</strong> en parcelas residenciales. Nos interesa una sola respuesta, que aplique a <u>todo o la mayor parte</u> del suelo en el<em> área de expansión</em>. Si ninguna respuesta aplica a aproximadamente el 80% del <u>suelo</u> del área de expansión, le pedimos que escriba una nota corta, explicando la situación en su ciudad. Si una pregunta no tiene sentido para usted, queremos saber porqué, para tener información precisa sobre su ciudad.</span></p>  <p>   <span style="font-size:12px;">Algunas preguntas pueden referirse a la<em> periferia</em> de la ciudad y no al área de expansión. La periferia se refiere a las tierras incluidas o quizá fuera del límite exterior del área de expansión, es decir, áreas en las cuales tiene lugar el más reciente desarrollo urbano/metropolitano en la actualidad.</span></p>  <p>   <span style="font-size:12px;">Empezamos con la Parte I.</span></p>  <div>   <a class="various fancybox.iframe" href="https://www.google.com/maps/d/u/0/embed?mid=zMhLaSs1bI9M.kb6YVP5NkORw&z=10&ll=11.17847,76.68364"><button>Ver mapa</button></a></div>  		es-AR
